"Phoebis sennae","2015-10-02 00:00:00 -0600","Cloudless Sulphur (Phoebis sennae)

2 October 2015: Visited and walked about at the Hagerman National Wildlife Refuge (HNWF) for the first time on October 2, 2015 and we came upon dozens of Cloudless Sulphur (Phoebis sennae) flying throughout the environs of the federal nature preserve located on the southeastern shores of Lake Texoma. We wish to thank and acknowledge Dr. Cliff Ivy who graciously made the IDentification for us on BugGuide. To access the ID of Cloudless Sulphur on BugGuide please go here: http://bugguide.net/node/view/1149440
